  要</span></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;min-height: 1em;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">对于通讯交通不发达的古代，网友调侃是“交通全靠走，通讯全靠吼”。所以，在这种情况下，又有人提出疑问：古代官员奔赴远方上任，如果被人伪造委任状冒充怎么办？</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">冒任官员这类事件在古代志怪小说中并不鲜见，在明末文言短篇小说集《虞初新志》中，记录了崇祯初年一位出任广东雷州的官员中途被截杀并冒充的故事：</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><section style=\"margin-left: 16px;margin-right: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">“雷于粤为最远郡。崇祯初，金陵人某，以部曹出守。舟入江遇盗。知其守也，杀之，并歼其从者，独留其妻女。以众中一最黠者为伪守，持牒往，而群诡为仆人，莫能察也。”</span></section><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">当时，广东雷州还属于较偏远地区，这位官员带着家眷在前来上任的路上，遇到一伙山贼打劫，官员和他的家人被杀害。这伙山贼的首领，利用官员留下的文书，来到雷州，接替了他的职务，神不知鬼不觉的在雷州做起了官，直到真正官员的儿子前来投奔，才露出马脚。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">而《西游记》中，唐僧的父亲陈光蕊也是在上任前被船夫刘洪杀害冒充，任职江州直到唐僧成人以后才东窗事发。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-croporisrc=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/laADTC8BCK7Ehkybv0vJUdKL7sVJ1qxtSLrTRAThAF1HbgVRelPy4z5EX1hst11nSed4J5TPDUKMk7LvQic0lqA/0?wx_fmt=jpeg\" data-cropx1=\"0\" data-cropx2=\"640.0000000000001\" data-cropy1=\"0\" data-cropy2=\"438.43416370106763\" data-ratio=\"0.6828125\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"640\" style=\"width: 562px; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">86版《西游记》中的唐僧父母</span><br></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">那么，志怪小说所演绎的冒任官员事件在现实中可能发生吗？</span></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;transform: rotateY(180deg);-webkit-transform: rotateY(180deg);-moz-transform: rotateY(180deg);-o-transform: rotateY(180deg);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 1 1 auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"border-top: 1px dashed rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: style=\"transform: rotateZ(45deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(45deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(45deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(45deg);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 9px;height: 9px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 222, 23);border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(255, 255, 255) 1px 1px 0px inset;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 1 auto;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(161, 121, 43);box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">官员赴任前都需要准备什么</strong></span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 1 1 auto;border-width: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"border-top: 1px dashed rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"transform: rotateZ(45deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(45deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(45deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(45deg);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 9px;height: 9px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 222, 23);border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(255, 255, 255) 1px 1px 0px inset;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">在古代，冒任夺官的高级骗子屡见不鲜，虽说如此，盗官这事实际操作起来，从官员赴任的手续上看，有相当的难度。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">古代官员调动一般是通过中央的程序调动和官凭赴任。官员一般不能在本地任职，</span><span style=\"font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif rgb>然而，那时没有照片以及完备的人事档案和调动记录，仅有备案的文件又存放于吏部，所以赖以验明正身的只有两样物件：委任状与身份证明，这是官员上任所需要的官凭。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">两份文件详细注明了赴任官员的基本情况，如姓名、籍贯、年龄、体貌特征等，同时还印有吏部的章印，而且委任状也经过专门设计。以唐代文书为例，委任状文书用的是金花五色绫纸，宋代用的是丝织花绫，加之设计精美，不是那么容易被仿冒。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-ratio=\"0.5954825462012321\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"487\" style=\"height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/laADTC8BCK4mSnypXicEnecS6dDVBpjPmTpIiaB0Bj6DsgT8tt5xMwQddgMo7a5WOsgYEBzf6w1JGt7bmG2Nt1oA/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">唐代文书</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">官员上任的另一个凭证叫</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">鱼</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">符，一个鱼状的物品，上边记载了一个人的基本信息，名字，简介，官品。类似的还有虎符、龟符、龙符和兔符，作用都是一样的。宋朝有牙牌和腰牌，也是官员用来证明身份的，上边刻有官员的姓名和官职等重要信息。而且，三品官员以上的鱼符是用金子打造的，三品和五品是用银子打造的，五品以下的官员是用铜材质打造的，这里面的规矩，</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">普通老百姓很难了解，一旦伪造很容易被拆穿。</span></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;\"><br></section><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">除了携带了不易复制的凭证，官员上任前的流程也在一定程度上增加了冒任难度。以</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">明清为例，授官惯例大概是这样：科举考试中，只有一甲的前三名，即状元、榜眼、探花能马上安排官职，其余的则分送各衙门办事，这种做法后来沿袭成一项制度。状元马上授予修撰</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（从六品）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">，榜眼和探花是编修</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（正七品）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">，也就是翰林。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">“朝考”之后，中央会选拔一批进士入翰林院，担任庶吉士。庶吉士并非正式官职，实际上相当于在翰林院实习，在翰林院里学习，称之为“选馆”。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">在这个过程中，无法进入翰林的进士们会走候补流程，被分派到中央各部和地方。无论等候分派的进士还是在外调动的官员，如果没有补授实缺则被纳入吏部候选，吏部将名单汇总，根据职位、资格等抽签，进而分发到某部或某省。</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">以清代为例</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">，</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">调动到地方的官员需要拿着</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">吏部凭证到省会等待差事，这时，</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">省会里的督抚</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">官员对于即将到各地任职的地方官开始了解和认识。所以，在这样一套流程下，即使一时冒名顶替成功，日后到省会办公也会露馅。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><section style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;align-items: center;display: flex;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;transform: rotateY(180deg);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 1 1 auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"border-top: 1px dashed rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"transform: rotateZ(45deg);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 9px;height: 9px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 222, 23);border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(255, 255, 255) 1px 1px 0px inset;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 1 auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(161, 121, 43);box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\">冒充的手法</strong></span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 1 1 auto;border-width: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"border-top: 1px dashed rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"transform: rotateZ(45deg);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 9px;height: 9px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 222, 23);border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(255, 255, 255) 1px 1px 0px inset;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">上有政策，下有对策。在信息不发达的古代，如果依然有人想冒充官员，都是怎么钻空子的呢？</span><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">一则是利用职务或身份之便。</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">宋太宗时，秦州节度判官李若愚之子李飞雄利用自身的家世，多次矫诏并冒充使者招摇撞骗，声势浩大且嚣张跋扈，肆意妄为到斩杀官员。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">一次，李飞雄去周至县看望岳父，临走时将其岳父的“官马”盗走。他骑着“官马”来到驿站“诈称使者”，驿站工作人员看他气焰嚣张，又骑着“官马”，便信以为真。李飞雄临行时，要求驿站派向导带路，此后，他每到一处都用这种办法，不但路越走越远，身边的随从也越来越多，包括陇州监军，吴山县尉等政府官员都成了李飞雄的随从。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">这批人跟着所谓的“使者”李飞雄，来到甘肃清水县。当时的清水是北宋边疆重镇，驻扎大批士兵。李飞雄竟不费吹灰之力就将当地驻军的主要将领抓了起来。这些边将，无一人敢反抗。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">李飞雄为了提高自己的可信度，还谎称曾在“晋王府”当差，是宋太宗的亲信，但是没想到被抓的边将中，有人曾在晋王府当差。李飞雄的骗局被揭穿，此人假意欲与李飞雄共事，结果设计将李飞雄抓获。</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></p><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-ratio=\"0.7460674157303371\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"445\" style=\"height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/laADTC8BCK4mSnypXicEnecS6dDVBpjPm1jUrysiaOBpB8Ubibkh1GpX9wdNUYY9AWPiabz3Xahic88SRvDDaSTNRSg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">宋太宗</span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">李飞雄招供后，被投入大牢。宋太宗大怒，下令将主犯李飞雄处死并夷灭三族，连带李飞雄行骗过程中第一个向导也被处死灭三族。同时所有被骗官员一律腰斩。此事还牵连了一桩冤案，当时北宋的乾州知州名为李若拙，和李飞雄的父亲李若愚并无关系，也因为此事被免官流放至海南，仅仅因为名字一字之差。</span></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">二是伪造一个假的身份。</span></strong><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">《明神宗实录》中记载，明朝万历年间，一个叫杨春的人，自称“杨参军把总”“崔都司委官”等多个官员身份，因为头衔太多，造假得太过分没人相信，又假借了戚继光之名广布明文征兵，还征募了四百多人，对当地的豪绅勒索恐吓，最后为明朝官方出面缉捕。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"></span></section><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">不管是李飞雄还是杨春，他们窃官时天下大抵承平，他们的行为也没有对统治秩序产生很大影响，而当中央王朝对地方掌控力不强时，窃官者就有更大的发挥空间，</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">而把这事做得最过火的，发生在元顺帝时期。</span></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">《元史》记载：“至元五年十一月戊辰，开封杞县人范孟反，伪传帝旨，杀河南行省平章政事月禄帖木儿、左丞劫烈、廉访使完者不花等，已而捕诛之。”</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">这件事在《庚申外史》中有比较详细的叙述。至元五年十一月</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（1339年）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">，河南有一个范孟端的小吏，出身河南杞县，一开始为内台知班。他郁郁不得志，又没有什么升职加薪的机会，因为看不惯达官贵人碌碌无为。有一日，他在墙上题了一首诗：</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">“人皆谓我不办事，天下办事有几人？袖里屠龙斩蛟手，埋没青锋二十春。”</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">然后就决定要杀官造反了。当时，很多蒙古人、色目人的官员汉语水平严重不过关，给了范孟端很好的冒充机会。一天晚上，范孟端和朋友霍八失等约定：“我在冬至那天在行省衙门当值，你们四人当以黄腊为丸弹状佩之，大摇大摆冒充成钦差，偷几匹马，半夜时分从范孟端看守的大门进去，坐到行省衙门公堂里，唤当值的掾吏来传圣旨……”</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">那一晚，当地行省官员大摆筵席喝得酩酊大醉，范孟端的计划照常进行。在传召来了致仕在家的河南廉访使段惟德之后，他就开始了表演，在醉醺醺的河南行省平章政事月禄帖木儿、左丞劫烈、理问金刚奴</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（正四品）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">、郎中完者秃黑的儿</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（从五品）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">、都事拜住</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（从七品）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">，河南廉访使秃满</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（正三品）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">，汴梁路总管撒思麻</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（正三品）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">、万户完者不花</span><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\">（正三品）</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">等一干高官面前，命令他们跪听圣旨。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">元朝自立国以来，皇位更迭频繁，动乱不断，行省官员对这种场面并没有太过惊异，但当他们服服帖帖的趴在地上接旨后，范孟端一行人就从后面拿着铁骨朵，锤死了这群高官，弃尸在后花园里。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">此后，范孟端以元顺帝的名义，封自己为河南都元帅，拘收了大小衙门印，自佩平章发兵虎符，调兵守城，封诸街巷中，不许居民往来；并封闭黄河大江渡船，隔绝南北，还调集了河南的各路兵马会合。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">一切工作完成后，范孟端回老家杞县祭祖，大张旗鼓长达五天。想起以前的仇人，就把行省各路衙门几十位“正官、首领官”传召进来，“斩于市”。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">此时，范孟端的好日子也快到头了。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">一个叫冯二舍的小官想巴结他，范孟端一不注意就露了马脚。当时，范孟端喝醉了，冯二舍问他：“能不能引见我见见朝廷官。”喝醉的范孟端，开始口不择言、夸下海口：“何者为朝廷官？我便是也。”冯二舍发觉其中不对，趁范孟端外出时，向他的上级镇抚司汇报范孟端可能是假使者的情况，范孟端和他几个同伙才被扑杀。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">仅仅是几个人和几把骨朵，就把元朝河南行省搅和得天翻地覆，杀害大批元朝高</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">官，这场景实在是魔幻又诡谲。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">有元一代，元朝政府对地方的控制能力一直很差。</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">行政机构的腐化，地方官员管理系统不甚完善，给了范孟端等人机会。</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">一旦中央政府对地方有较强控制力的时候，这一套就很难奏效了。</span></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></p><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">历史上即便是庸官，也有一定的文化水平，在赴任和后续与官员接洽时，也有一定的应对能力，加上古代读书人的圈子并不大，许多官员上任以前，也要经过培训，明清时期的翰林和庶吉士就类似于官员上任前的管培，不置身于这个环境中，很难进行长期伪装。</span></span></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;\"></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;margin-top: 15px;margin-bottom: 15px;text-align: center;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;transform: rotateY(180deg);-webkit-transform: rotateY(180deg);-moz-transform: rotateY(180deg);-o-transform: rotateY(180deg);box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 1 1 auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"border-top: 1px dashed rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"transform: rotateZ(45deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(45deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(45deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(45deg);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"margin-right: 0%;margin-left: 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 9px;height: 9px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 222, 23);border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(255, 255, 255) 1px 1px 0px inset;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 1 auto;padding-right: 10px;padding-left: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><strong style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(161, 121, 43);box-sizing: border-box;\">花押、备案——朝廷的防范手段</span></strong><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;height: auto;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"align-items: center;display: flex;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 1 1 auto;border-width: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"border-top: 1px dashed rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section></section><section style=\"display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: auto;flex: 0 0 auto;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"transform: rotateZ(45deg);-webkit-transform: rotateZ(45deg);-moz-transform: rotateZ(45deg);-o-transform: rotateZ(45deg);box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"display: inline-block;width: 9px;height: 9px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(255, 222, 23);border-width: 1px;border-radius: 0px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-shadow: rgb(255, 255, 255) 1px 1px 0px inset;line-height: 0;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><h3 style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></h3><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">为了让官员顺利赴任，中央政府也有相关的防范手段，比如明朝的花押制度，最大限度的从根源上防止冒官事件发生。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">花押，就是古人的个性签名，相传最早起源于钟繇，（唐）韦续《墨薮》中里提到：“行书，正小之谓也，钟繇谓之‘行押书’。”在魏晋南北朝时，押字就开始被使用。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">唐代的文书墨迹中已经见有花押作为个人独特的信约标记，但兴盛起来还是在元朝。元抄花押也称元押、元戳，花押印的形状多为长方，一般上刻楷书姓氏，下刻蒙古文或花押，其目的在于取信，使人不易辨认摹仿。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.5942549371633752\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"557\" style=\"font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont,; max-width: 600px\" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif center normal rgb border-box break-word visible auto src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/laADTC8BCK4mSnypXicEnecS6dDVBpjPmIr47qJF2jZ8CcCticria4lt5ZlWeyyic4tamOBUYTf9AEDGBzus7X71OQ/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">明朝对元朝盛行的花押有一定传承，开始用于公文书写，明朝郎瑛在《七修类稿》的 “押字”条下对明朝的花押制度是这样记录的：“国朝押字之制，虽未必名，而上下多用一画，盖取地平天成之意。凡释褐入官者，皆以吏部画字三日，以验异时文移之真伪。故京都有卖花字者，随人意欲，必有宛转藏顿，苟知所本，则当以名，庶不乖古义云。”</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">当官员入仕为官时，需要行文到吏部，这样一来上级以及交接的官员应当可以通过花押对文书真伪进行验证，笔迹的验证也逐渐成为赴任官员验明正身的一种方式。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.6686567164179105\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"335\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 429px !important; visibility: visible !important; height: auto !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/laADTC8BCK4mSnypXicEnecS6dDVBpjPmzstniaoG2EWFHe6JsOD8NFf5VAkScVspjicZaJEsVh9CC3cgPLnZTZzg/640?wx_fmt=png\"></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">《绣春刀》中身着四品官袍的崇祯皇帝</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><p style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">到了清代，对于公文上的花押也要每年核验比对，所谓“岁暮封印，旧制，遇紧要文移，于年月两旁，硃写印信遵封。上司牌票，则刻本官花押，钤盖年月上”</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">正是如此。</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">除此之外，清代知府级官员可以直接上密折向皇帝汇报情况，上下情通达，即便出现假冒情况，也会被迅速发现抓捕。</span></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">明清时期，中央政府的种种举措和实际情况的限制，很多时候将冒任官员的事件发生限制在志怪小说中，而现实中如果进行实操，哪怕一时成功，也不可能是长久之策。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">直到清末民初时期，国内环境陷入动荡，地方自行其事，夺官冒任事件又频繁发生。</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">电影《让子弹飞》中，曾在军中任职的绿林侠匪张牧之，在劫持了买官上任的老汤以后，冒名赴任的官员走马上任鹅城。</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">这并不是一个典型的冒官现象，张牧之亦官亦匪，相对了解地方政府的运行规则，同时挟持了老汤，也避免了因揭发而暴露的</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">情况</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">。</span></p><p style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;\"><br></p><section style=\"margin-right: 8px;margin-left: 8px;white-space: normal;text-align: center;\"><img class=\"rich_pages js_insertlocalimg\" data-croporisrc=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/laADTC8BCK4mSnypXicEnecS6dDVBpjPmiaHdN6LA01RDq8awV2YsGg6Y9jIkjIYwzbUSt0YSiapevZmZt1Yq4oBw/0?wx_fmt=jpeg\" 16px;\">在没有秩序可言的乱世，冒任也显得不那么突兀。而纵观整个中国古代历史，冒任官员属于“欺君之罪”，是连姓名相仿都容易受到株连的罪过，如此高的犯罪成本，古人一般不会轻易铤而走险的。</span></p><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: !important;\">在“华星”，陈淑芬为张国荣买回《MONICA》版权，拿下“十大金曲”。还找喜多郎作曲，为梅艳芳定制《似水流年》，一炮走红。可以说，要没有陈淑芬出力，中国香港两大金嗓，未必会这么快走上巨星宝座。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/SKDZgibAnFCEl3r0MkDBNE3DX4e6gLhXichQE0PuxljFU1lRq5rnichtvvzW9cG92tdaXrZjJ8nUVy7iboGcibVDXicA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1984年“十大金曲奖”上的张国荣</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1985年，中国内地听歌，全靠村头大喇叭。最受欢迎的还是蒋大为老师《在那桃花盛开的地方》。</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">那时</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">就没有“流行”一说，安个好听的名字叫“通俗”。1986年倒是有个“孔雀杯·通俗歌曲大奖赛”。能拿奖的，都是地方文艺骨干，比如成方圆，</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">同年参赛的，还有北京歌舞团的崔健。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">在民族、美声主流影响下，80年代最硬的舞台，只有“青歌赛”。<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那是首个国家级声乐比赛。参赛者都是各地文工团的人。参赛前，得先在地方团唱出名，才能去顶级舞台PK。</strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">开赛第二年，设立“通俗唱法”。一度爆红的韦唯、毛阿敏还有蔡国庆，正是靠这一组别成了主流歌手。后来拿奖的，还有几个初代流行歌手，毛宁、孙悦、林依轮。青赛历史上，有些歌手奖都没拿。比如韩红5次未进决赛，据说还有个成都姑娘，四川赛区选拔都没进，</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">就是李宇春。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.7060931899641577\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"558\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 558px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/SKDZgibAnFCEl3r0MkDBNE3DX4e6gLhXicaDb5V2lEdWNgwNVAAEWRQC8POBqQRnphFh3fcqUTLO3bEMyD4sGP2Q/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1985年“孔雀杯”的入选歌手名单</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那年代，上了青歌赛，意味着前途无限。1986年，天津歌手许丽丽因拿下通俗组第一名，回城时被父老乡亲夹道欢迎，地方直接奖励两居室和18英寸彩电。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">然而，80年代末，港台流行风徐徐吹来，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">躁动的灵魂很多，漂亮的声线大把，但能发光的舞台，仅此一个。</strong>全国卫视加起来不到10个，且都没上星。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">拿乐评人金兆钧的话说就是：</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“当时没别的，这是歌手出道的唯一渠道。”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">无奈之下，其他好声音，只能唱歌厅。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);min-height: 1em;max-inline-size: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-family: 微软雅黑, \" microsoft yahei arial sans-serif rgb center border-box break-word none><span style=\"font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><em style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);max-width: 100%;max-inline-size: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;outline: none 0px !important;\">02.</span></em></span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果说晚会、青歌赛是登上主流舞台的唯一途径，那么歌厅就是民间高手发光发热的绝佳场所。80年代末90年代初，北上广这三个先锋改革城市，出现了大大小小的歌厅。</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">北京</span></span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">尤以“和平House”为盛。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">许多好嗓子，就在这些歌厅驻唱。比较著名的，广州有杨钰莹、陈明，北京这边，韩磊在“香港美食城”，满文军在“台湾饭店”。后来周迅赴京，在歌厅唱《亲密爱人》，一晚上能赚150块钱。这么高的收入，对会唱歌的人，自然是不能不去。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\"> </span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.5802469135802469\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1134\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/SKDZgibAnFCEl3r0MkDBNE3DX4e6gLhXic2rYLy0Ta8KlbymO1Siax68BicxgXItfcJ20PR4jhCKiaUeQXPjmiaduOBA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">当年著名夜场之一，卡萨布兰卡</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">不过队伍里，也有混得一般的。</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">众所周知，黄渤当年在青岛，也是响当当的人物。后来青岛无法满足梦想，就组了个“蓝色风沙”，全国各地走穴。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">黄渤得到音乐自信，主要是初中元旦晚会唱了《再回首》，赢得全校师生赞叹。后来他参加“龙城杯中学生卡拉OK比赛”，为学校捧回一个三等奖。赛后，举办方搞了个夏令营。就在那里，黄渤遇到了高虎。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">从此，黄渤梦想做一名真正的歌手。以他的资质，上不了“青歌赛”，恰逢歌厅鼎盛，开始频繁走穴。走出青岛，黄渤雄心勃勃，拉着一支队伍，打算闯出一片天地。结果天南海北，三教九流，被坑数次。为了多赚点钱，他跑去东北演出时，假装是香港明星，结果坐公交被观众撞见。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">人家问你不是港星吗，他说：</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">“我这是来体验生活的。”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">有次去南京，对方说好给2000块。表演完，人跑了。离开南京前夜，金陵大寒，黄渤心也结冰，不知这种日子，何时是个头。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">驻唱时，黄渤这种长得不帅的，什么刁难都有。啤酒，人家要你喝十瓶，你得喝，人家叫你唱《青藏高原》，你得唱。场子稍微一冷，老板就让你走人。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这也是歌厅歌手和晚会歌手的差距。</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">许巍当年在南方演歌厅，受不了这个，扭头回西安组了“飞乐队”。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">杨坤也吃了不少脾气上的亏。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">杨坤辍学很早，幸好参加包头市一个唱歌比赛，才把梦想寄托在音乐上。由于嗓子好，他考上了当地武警文工团。团友工资几十块，他跑去驻唱，月入三四千。</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">但杨坤并不满足在歌厅驻唱。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">抱着无限憧憬，手持800块现金，他跑到了北京。结果在保利大厦唱歌，没两天就被炒了。幸好一司机不要他钱，给他拉到“卡萨布兰卡”。杨坤用仅剩的100元点歌上台。沙宝亮一听，惊了。赶紧跟老板说：</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">“必须把这小子留下来。”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">但因为脾气倔，不买客人账，不混圈子，没多久，他又被老板炒了。之后几年，他在北京睡地下室、睡澡堂子。前前后后算起来，北漂期间，杨坤搬家55次。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.5404255319148936\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"940\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/SKDZgibAnFCEl3r0MkDBNE3DX4e6gLhXicY4l7bYpo2glzsHaaxZS1F68XokMy5vljnRSvv7jZqodSvPDTB2vpqQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">驻唱时期的杨坤</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1992年，杨坤去北京前，团友曾在厕所里给他录过自制带。带子里，他唱了《再回首》。团友开玩笑说了这样一段话：</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">“大家好，下面让我为你介绍我的朋友，杨坤。几年来的舞厅伴唱生涯，使他对人生失去了信心，他为没人为他写歌而苦恼，有如一只海上漂泊的孤舟。他绝望了，他悲伤了。看着过往的人群，看着明亮的华灯，他流泪了。</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);letter-spacing: normal;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">他最大的痛苦是老唱别人的歌，最大的愿望，是人们会唱他的歌。</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;max-width: 100%;color: rgb(217, 33, 66);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><em style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></em></span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1992年，很多歌厅歌手和杨坤一样痛苦、绝望。他们更希望能站上真正的舞台，唱属于自己的歌。</span></span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">但从一个</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">普通夜场卖唱，成为一名专业歌手，这中间的路，何其难也？</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">好在这时，时代给了他们机会。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\"> </span><br></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(204, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-family: 微软雅黑, \" microsoft yahei arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word><em style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(204, 0, 0);max-width: 100%;max-inline-size: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;outline: none 0px !important;\">03.</span></em></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1992年，改革之风越来越盛。《东方时空》一度花200万搞了个“金曲栏目”，开始推广流行歌。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">大气候中，唱片公司来了。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那一年，北京最贵的涉外公寓写字楼京城大厦，“正大国际音乐制作中心”作为内地首家中外合资唱片公司成立。公司直接参照国外模式，请写《月亮代表我的心》的孙仪当副总，请香港的鲍比达来做音乐总监。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">最早被正大捧红的，是孙悦。</span></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">孙悦早年在哈尔滨文工团，后来参加青歌赛入京。当年她最大一笔收入，是帮人唱翻唱磁带，拿了5000块钱。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">一个偶然机会，孙悦遇到了刘青老师写的《祝你平安》。刘老师写过不少名曲，给那姐写过《山不转水转》。《祝你平安》，最早本来是那英唱的。孙悦听到这首歌后，想再唱一个自己的版本，就把它买了。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><section><qqmusic class=\"js_editor_qqmusic qqmusic_iframe BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.5952\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1250\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; width: 677px !important; visibility: visible !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/SKDZgibAnFCEl3r0MkDBNE3DX4e6gLhXicbftthONQ5lLmphoYegOibEia0UsiajmaovKicO7fZVbUljwiciaXIuzeSd4A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">这才叫一个时代的记忆</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">果不其然，这首歌很快横扫各大电台，登上央视。孙悦也在一夜间成为最受欢迎的歌手。</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">到哪儿表演，都是压轴。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1994年，内地流行乐井喷。北方有高晓松他们的校园民谣，南方有以杨钰莹为代表的广州军。粤军全靠陈小奇。1992年，在音乐人陈小奇的牵头下，广州成立内地第一个音乐企划部。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">可以说，正是在陈小奇、黄小茂、孙仪等业内人的推扶下，才有了94年流行乐坛一时荣光，并为内地唱片业奠定了基础。此后，更多的唱片公司相继成立。那些早年无法登上主流舞台、只能在夜场卖唱、但同样拥有一副好嗓子的民间歌手们，终于多了一条成为“专业歌手”的道路。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb center border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(204, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-family: 微软雅黑, \" microsoft yahei arial sans-serif rgb border-box break-word><em style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;color: rgb(204, 0, 0);max-width: 100%;max-inline-size: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;outline: none 0px !important;\">04.</span></em></strong></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 16px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><br></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">也不知是缺运气，还是缺实力，黄渤最后心灰意冷回了青岛。当年他在北京跑夜场，突然被一家饭店叫去替唱。问了才知道，另一位歌手参赛去了。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">那时，黄渤每天骑车赶场。一天又一天，钱是够。但你看不到希望，不知还要唱多久。难不成在酒吧干一辈子？</span><span style=\"color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;\">无奈之下，只好回青岛。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">杨坤那边更惨。1992年到北京时，他想像日后的孙悦那样，拿到一首歌，一夜走红。结果等了几年，没钱买，只好跟一帮北漂学作曲，自己写了《无所谓</span><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">》。这首歌1997年就录好了，2002年才红。此前，他的小样无数次被唱片公司丢进垃圾桶，家里攒了30本合同，每天只能吃一顿木须肉。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">以至于走红后，杨坤在首体唱《无所谓》，看着台下观众，泪眼婆娑。</span></p><p style=\"margin: 5px 8px;max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(34, 34, 34);font-size: 16px;letter-spacing: normal;box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"> </span></p><section><qqmusic class=\"js_editor_qqmusic qqmusic_iframe js_uneditable custom_select_card\" musicid=\"1734508\" mid=\"000TuOFf1bys4V\"
